<div id="review_45910560" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/45910560" />
    <a title="Shannon" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2016128-shannon"><img alt="Shannon" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1572638169p2/2016128.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/45910560?book_show_action=true">Feb 10, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shannon" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shannon" href="/user/show/2016128-shannon">Shannon</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=owned">owned</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=2010">2010</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=werewolves">werewolves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=color-red">color-red</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=demons">demons</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer45910560" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1114651344219059539">A wonderful series that could use a smidge more romance although I'm enjoying the slow build-up between Mercy and her men. The only thing is though, has this love-triangle turned into a love-square? <br/><br/><i>Stefan, Mercy's Mystery Machine bus-driving vampire friend, asks her for a favor. She owed him after the events of the last book so she reluctantly agrees. Mercy goes with Stefan to a hotel to meet with a vampire that entered the area without checking in with the queen first. Stefan asks Mercy to acc</i></span>
  <span id="freeText1114651344219059539" style="display:none">A wonderful series that could use a smidge more romance although I'm enjoying the slow build-up between Mercy and her men. The only thing is though, has this love-triangle turned into a love-square? <br /><br /><i>Stefan, Mercy's Mystery Machine bus-driving vampire friend, asks her for a favor. She owed him after the events of the last book so she reluctantly agrees. Mercy goes with Stefan to a hotel to meet with a vampire that entered the area without checking in with the queen first. Stefan asks Mercy to accompany him as a coyote in a harness and to act as his pet, she's merely supposed to be part of his costume so he can intimidate the other vampire. Once they get to the hotel though they realize that things aren't as they seem. The hotel is all but empty and Mercy smells something amiss. The creature they meet there isn't just any vampire and Mercy, Stefan, and the rest of her close friends all get thrown into a conflict with a being more evil than they could have imagined.</i><br /><br />This series's best quality is the characters. They're very well-developed and they feel real; I want to know and I also care about what's going to happen to them. Mercy is likable and down-to-earth; she's the type of girl you'd want to be friends with and have at your back. I'm not sure how I feel about Samuel, but at least he's there to make sure Mercy is safe, even though he really just wants her to have his kids. <b>Adam, though, is delicious.</b> I love how he takes care of his women (Mercy and Jesse) and also manages his pack as a true Alpha. I think he's finally figured out how to deal with Mercy and get through to her without her feeling controlled by him. I hope the next book proves this and their relationship moves forward.<br /><br />I normally like vampire stories better but I have to say this is my favorite werewolf series. <b>I like Briggs's wolves and I think she does one of the best jobs at describing their behavior and making them seem real.</b> <br /><br />On top of the great characterization of the main characters, the side characters do their job of fleshing out the story as well. <b>I normally have a hard time when there's a huge cast but Briggs does a great job of describing them and giving them all a unique personality.</b> And even if she's reintroducing a character we didn't spend a lot of time with she gives a bit of information that jogs the reader's memory. If only all authors would do this! There's been so many series I've gotten frustrated with because I'd forgotten who a character was and I'd sit their with it in the back of my mind trying to figure out who they were and this would kind of ruin the story for me.<br /><br />The villain in this book was actually scary too! I'm not embarrassed to say that I was home alone reading this at night and when I got to a certain part I actually got kind of jumpy. My house is old and makes all kinds of noises and I <i>know</i> this but I kept thinking back to a certain scene in this book and freaking myself out. <br /><br />A great second book and a great story in general. I can't wait to read more about Mercy and her friends!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1114651344219059539" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/145835928" />
    <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352609417p2/2489554.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/145835928?book_show_action=true">Feb 04, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog">Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Urban Fantasy fans, Fans of Alpha werewolves and vampires</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=lgbt">lgbt</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=drinks-on-me">drinks-on-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=king-of-the-harem">king-of-the-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-urban-fantasy">genre-urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=my-hottie-harem">my-hottie-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-i-go-rabid-over">books-i-go-rabid-over</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=covers-to-covet">covers-to-covet</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer145835928" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2917566932607489891"><b> Minor Spoilers!</b><br/><br/><i> Blood Bound</i>, the second book in the Mercy Thompson series was definitely better than the first! I thought the story was much more engaging in this one. There was a purpose straight from the beginning and of course, I can’t complain since Stefan has a considerable amount of page time!<br/><br/>Mercy, my new favourite heroine, finds herself in a bit of a situation involving the seethe and a certain demon-riding vampire named Cory Littleton. The guy ended up with a wuss name, but this creep </span>
  <span id="freeText2917566932607489891" style="display:none"><b> Minor Spoilers!</b><br /><br /><i> Blood Bound</i>, the second book in the Mercy Thompson series was definitely better than the first! I thought the story was much more engaging in this one. There was a purpose straight from the beginning and of course, I can’t complain since Stefan has a considerable amount of page time!<br /><br />Mercy, my new favourite heroine, finds herself in a bit of a situation involving the seethe and a certain demon-riding vampire named Cory Littleton. The guy ended up with a wuss name, but this creep is scary as fuck! The scene where he was pressed up against Mercy’s bedroom window, scratching the glass with his teeth made me want to go screaming for Sam. But Mercy handles her fear well. She does this countless times within this book, playing detective and using her connections to her advantage. Not only she is capable, but she’s smart as hell too!<br /><br />Briggs knows how to tease me. She loves ending books with the Mercy-Adam-Samuel love triangle. My heart broke when Samuel revealed the truth about what happened when he was in Texas. Aww, the poor guy! And then there’s the fact that he kisses Mercy! TWICE!!<br /><br />And what about that work-out scene with Adam? That scene served two purposes. One, readers get to read about a sweaty Adam. Cue swoons. And two, it furthers the storyline with the dom/sub issue between Mercy and Adam. I don’t see it as a problem since neither of them can control themselves around each other. <br /><br />I have no idea who Mercy is going to choose because I adore both wolves equally! I don’t think Mercy is a girl who’ll leads men on. But if there’s one thing that’s got me hooked about this series, it’s the love triangle! I can’t help myself!<br /><br />But this book wasn’t without its imperfections! I thought some scenes dragged on a little too long, such as Mercy’s second visit to Stefan’s menagerie. Nevertheless, this book was damn entertaining and since <i> River-Marked</i> releases tomorrow, I don’t have to wait long to find out what happens!!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2917566932607489891" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

And I was about to after 70% of this book (this book could have been shorter, btw) w</span>
  <span id="freeText5466767723478051595" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418050973ra/12650461.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><u>My notes reading this book:</u><br><i>5% - Boring<br>20% - I already know that<br>50% - Still boring<br>65% - Hmm... okay.<br>70% - Cool!<br>90% - This chick is awesome!!<br>100% - Why all I can remember is being bored?</i><br><br><b>I can definitely see there's something great going on with this series</b>. I love UF, great female characters, action-packed scenes... so why is this not working for me? <br><br>I'd love to say this series just didn't work for me and move on. And I was about to after 70% of this book (this book could have been shorter, btw) when finally exciting things happened. The villain was a complete win and Stefan freaking adorable. Mercy's decision of <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[go hunting Andre <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> was so welcomed, I really needed her to be on her own, making the hard decisions. Stop just letting shit happen to you, girl and take control. <br><br>I think my problem is I'm still trying to connect with the characters. I can't describe Mercy. She's what? stubborn? brave? fragile? intelligent? She's had a hard past and she knows nothing (doesn't seem to care anyway) about what she is and what she can do. She's excusing the wolves' behavior 30% of this book.<br><br><b>
  <i>"It wasn't his fault, werewolf instincts are very strong."</i>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403158189ra/10050730.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I'm getting tired of that shit.<br><br> LOVE SQUARE, YOU SAY?<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I love Stefan but really?? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Samuel is up, he's down. One day he's all about possessiveness, next day he's crying? He wants to leave but not before an unforgettable kiss? You know, he could do us all a favor and just go home. Why is he here in the first place? How does it work that the one who used to be the love of your life is living in your trailer, sleeping next to your bedroom and checking on how you smell all the time? You can't even have a private conversation!<br><br>SHE WON'T HAVE YOUR BABIES, YOU JERK<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418065856i/12659823.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Adam is the most decent option in this mess. He protects Mercy, points for that and his fierce love for Jessie melt my insides. My problem is how they treat Mercy. With werewolves, if a weak male mates with a strong female, she has to tune it down and be submissive because of his mate. Not fair at all. If a dominant male is in front of her, he can use his dominant effect on her and she will feel the <i>need</i> to please him. When Mercy asks Adam about that he excuses himself with the old "Not my fault! you make me feel this way!" card.<br><br>Never read a book about skinwalkers so I can't say much about that but I'd like a more proactive Mercy in the future, I respect her more now and I need to see her as the strong heroine I know she is.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1284959923" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1520294084807341374">When a new vampire enters the area without paying his respects, Mercy's vampire friend Stefan asks her to provide him with back up while he lays down the law. What they discover is a whole lot more than either of them can handle –– a demonically possessed sorcerer who has been turned into a vampire. As the carnage increases Mercy, Stefan and the werewolves from the trip-city area join forces to hunt down the demon-vampire before the demon takes over and the real carnage begins. </span>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">
          

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review1284959923">
  <td colspan="2">

<span id="freeTextContainer3651011467392542276"><b>Audio: 5 STARS!<br/>Story: 4 STARS!</b> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Sarcasm, I found, makes terror more bearable.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> I love Mercy and her steady, even-tempered ways. No matter what she faces - and this installment was <b>
  <u>SCARY</u>
</b> - she always tries to do the right thing. <br/><br/>There's still no romance so I can't rate it higher, but I'm really coming to enjoy this PNR world that Patricia Briggs has created. On to the next!</span>

  <span id="freeText6297926506827552859" style="display:none">This is where Mercy‘s story gets really interesting for me.<br /><br /><i>“I was already a freak, a shapeshifter not tied to the moon who turned into a coyote. Neither human nor werewolf nor fae. I didn’t like thinking I might be even odder than I’d thought.“</i><br /><br />I like the plot of this second Mercy novel. It‘s believable and doesn‘t feel as convoluted as the Alpa &amp; Omega novels I read before this. The plot makes sense. The vampires are scary.<br /><br />The beginning was a little too much recounting and summarizing of the first book for my taste. <br /><br />And, again, amazing how little I remembered of the story!<br /><br />What Samuel and Stefan go through and how they interact with Mercy also works for me. I get it. Stefan, not so much, he seems to be a little arbitrary and insta-something. But I enjoyed this enough to stick to my previous 5-star rating. I loved Ms. Hanna!<br /><br />————<br />Chronological reading order and progress for my Mercyverse re-read:<br />- <s>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/71811.Moon_Called__Mercy_Thompson___1_" title="Moon Called (Mercy Thompson, #1) by Patricia Briggs" rel="nofollow noopener">Moon Called</a>
</s>, ★★★★★, 1st Mercy novel<br />- <i>extra</i>-<s>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22083139.Patricia_Briggs__Mercy_Thompson_Moon_Called_Vol__1" title="Patricia Briggs' Mercy Thompson Moon Called Vol. 1 by Patricia Briggs" rel="nofollow noopener">Patricia Briggs' Mercy Thompson: Moon Called Vol. 1</a>
</s>, ★★★☆☆, comic adaptation of the same...<br />- <s>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5393637.Alpha___Omega__Alpha___Omega___0_5_" title="Alpha &amp; Omega (Alpha &amp; Omega, #0.5) by Patricia Briggs" rel="nofollow noopener">Alpha &amp; Omega</a>
</s>, ★★★★☆, novella, start of the Alpha &amp; Omega spin-off<br />- <s>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8141390.Cry_Wolf__Alpha___Omega___1_" title="Cry Wolf (Alpha &amp; Omega, #1) by Patricia Briggs" rel="nofollow noopener">Cry Wolf</a>
</s>, ★★★★☆, 1st Alpha &amp; Omega novel<br />- <s>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8130498.Hunting_Ground__Alpha___Omega___2_" title="Hunting Ground (Alpha &amp; Omega, #2) by Patricia Briggs" rel="nofollow noopener">Hunting Ground</a>
</s>, ★★★★☆, 2nd Alpha &amp; Omega novel<br />- <s>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11599178.Blood_Bound__Mercy_Thompson___2_" title="Blood Bound (Mercy Thompson, #2) by Patricia Briggs" rel="nofollow noopener">Blood Bound</a>
</s>, ★★★★★, 2nd Mercy novel<br />- <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11713973.Iron_Kissed__Mercedes_Thompson___3_" title="Iron Kissed (Mercedes Thompson, #3) by Patricia Briggs" rel="nofollow noopener">Iron Kissed</a> next...<br /><br />Complete time-line for the "Mercyverse", including the short stories:<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.patriciabriggs.com/books/timeline.shtml">http://www.patriciabriggs.com/books/t...</a><br />————<br /><br />1st time read, 2008:<br /><br />Mercy is special. She's not a shapeshifter from the old world, but rather a walker from the new one. And as such vampires don't hold a thrall over her. Good enough for her undead friend to take her along to a possibly dangerous meeting with the new vampire in town. She's going undercover, too, as her shapeshifted self - a coyote.<br />Obviously things go downhill quickly from there and get messy. Very entertaining, read it on a weekend on my sofa, couldn't put it down! Second in series.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13933123631541356320">Blood Bound is just an amazing book, and Mercy Thompson an amazing series. From the very first pages of the book, I am constantly hooked to the story.</span>

<div id="review_599676932" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/599676932" />
    <a title="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet"><img alt="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1387046887p2/13567836.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/599676932?book_show_action=true">Apr 25, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘" href="/user/show/13567836-elise-a-k-a-ryder-s-pet">Elise ✘ a.k.a Ryder&#39;s Pet ✘</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6282698-blood-bound">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer599676932" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8343717717365166747"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*Still Too Much Information*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote> <br/><b>
  <u>Second re-read: 03.07.2019</u>
</b><br/>The second book in the series centers around Volkswagen mechanic and a walker (a magical being with the power to shift into a coyote at will), <b> Mercedes ‘Mercy’ Athena Thompson</b>. Mercy has a foot in all sorts of species; friends with a cop, sorta/sorta not friends with a vampire, her former boss a fae, her roommate a werewolf and let's not forget her neighbor is an Alpha werewolf. When said vampire checks in a favor, Mercy</span>
  <span id="freeText8343717717365166747" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*Still Too Much Information*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote> <br><b>
  <u>Second re-read: 03.07.2019</u>
</b><br>The second book in the series centers around Volkswagen mechanic and a walker (a magical being with the power to shift into a coyote at will), <b> Mercedes ‘Mercy’ Athena Thompson</b>. Mercy has a foot in all sorts of species; friends with a cop, sorta/sorta not friends with a vampire, her former boss a fae, her roommate a werewolf and let's not forget her neighbor is an Alpha werewolf. When said vampire checks in a favor, Mercy ends up in more trouble than she planned. Then there's also the two men in her life who wants her... What to do? Nothing, as Mercy tends to avoid emotions.<br><br>Overall, it's a nice read. It is, but it's just too long, too much information and takes too long to get to the point. <b>There's also the huge problem that I feel disconnected with all the characters</b>. The thing is, I can't connect with Mercy simply because she hides things, even from herself, because she doesn't want to admit things. So we're all kinda left on the outside looking in, with only a few hints that there's more, but Mercy shuts it down and says she's think about it later. This is a huge problem for me as I <i>
  <b>need</b>
</i> to connect with the character in order to enjoy myself. Also, I do like how strong willed Mercy is, but is it so wrong to submit sometimes?<br><br>A question though; which of the supernatural creatures are at the top of the food chain? Is it the vampires? Because the werewolves seems a bit scared of them...? No one wants war because the werewolves outnumber the vampires. And the fae doesn't seem all that hard to kill.... so who is the big bad? <br><br><b><u>Other Characters</u>:</b><br><i>The list is long so I put it in a spoilers tag.</i><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[→ <b>Adam Hauptman</b>, the Alpha of the local werewolf pack (the Columbia Basin Pack), and his human daughter, <b>Jessica ‘Jesse’ Tamarind Hauptman</b> (15).<br>→ <b>Samuel ‘Sam’ Llewellyn Cornick</b>, his father, <b>Bran ‘The Marrok’ Cornick</b>, and his brother, <b>Charles Cornick</b>, a financial genius. In the US, all the packs follow the Marrok, a title taken from the name of one of King Arthur’s knights who was a werewolf. The Marrok and his pack have oversight of all the werewolves in North America. Bran's mate, <b>Leah</b>. Samuel is a medical doctor.<br>→ <b>Siebold ‘Zee’ Adelbertsmiter</b> of the Black Forest, Mercy's former boss, had retired when he sold her the place, but he’d come out once in a while to “keep his hand in.” He's also a Metallzauber/gremlin (fae).<br>→ <b>Medea</b>, Mercy's cat.<br>→ <b>Stefan ‘the Soldier’ Uccello</b>, a vampire and a somewhat friend of Mercy.<br>→ <b>Elizaveta Arkadyevna Vyshnevetskaya</b>, the cleanup crew leader. She was the most powerful witch in the Pacific Northwest. Her grandson, <b>Robert</b>.<br>→ <b>Tony Montenegro</b> (33 or so), a cop and Mercy's friend.<br>→ <b>Darryl Zao</b>, Adam’s second. He was a Ph.D. engineer working at the Pacific Northwest Laboratories in some sort of government hush-hush project. <b>Auriele</b>, a chemistry teacher at Richland High and Darryl’s mate.<br>→ <b>Warren</b>, one of the good guys, a hero, Mercy's favorite in Adam's pack. Warren is also Adam's best friend and most trusted in the pack, and his third. He was also a lone wolf; simply because he's gay and most of the werewolves in power in the US had been born in a time when homosexuality was anathema, even punishable by death in some places. <br>→ <b>Kyle Brooks</b>, Warren’s current lover and a divorce lawyer.<br>→ <b>Ben</b>, a werewolf in Adam's pack. British.<br>→ <b>Margi</b>, Mercy's mother, <b>Curt</b>, Mercy's stepfather.<br>→ <b>Tad</b>, Mercy's old assistant and Zee's son.<br>→ <b>Signora Marsilia</b>, Mistress of the Mid-Columbia Seethe (vampire).<br>→ <b>Mary Jo</b>, a firefighter with the Kennewick FD, and pack member to Adam.<br>→ <b>Sylvia Sandoval</b> and her son, <b>Gabriel Sandoval</b> (16). Zee fixed her car and in exchange, Gabriel will work for Mercy.<br>→ <b>Cory Littleton</b>, a vampire sorcerers who let's himself be possessed by a demon.<br>→ <b>Andre ‘the Courtier’</b>, a vampire and left hand to the Mistress (Stefan is her right hand). <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Mercy kills him at the end of the book. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>→ <b>Daniel</b>, a new vampire made by Andre, though he was Stefan's when he was human. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Killed by Ben but it was Littleton fault as he controlled Ben. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>→ <b>Wulfe ‘the Wizard’</b>, a vampire who looks like a teenager.<br>→ <b>Tom Black/John Beckworth</b>, a reporter/an investigative journalist. His daughter, <b>Kara</b>, survived an attack from a werewolf at the age of 10, now 3 years later her father locks her up every full moon.<br>→ <b>Honey</b>, and her mate-and-husband, a plumbing contractor, <b>Peter Jorgenson</b>, werewolves in Adam's pack.<br>→ <b>Uncle Mike</b>, owner of a bar/tavern meant for the fae.<br>→ <b>Naomi</b> and <b>Rachel</b>, bloodgivers/sheeps to Stefan.<br>→ <b>Estelle ‘the Teacher’</b> and <b>Bernard</b>, old vampires belonging to the Mistress. Two of the few vampires strong enough to live on their own. The others being Stefan, Andre and Wulfe. Of the five most powerful vampires, only Stefan and Andre are truly Marsili's.<br>→ Mrs. <b>Marjorie Hanna</b>, a ghost. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Never trust a mechanic who drives new cars. They're either charging too much money for their work, or they can't keep an old car running - maybe both.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br><b>Genre</b>: - (Adult) Urban Fantasy (M/F)<br><b>Series</b>: - Series, Book Two.<br><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes and no. As Mercy avoids feelings it doesn't feel like a love triangle. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes, for now? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Favorite character?</b> - Adam Hauptman.<br><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - Sure.<br><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Sure.<br><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - It's me... I do love re-reading. <br><b>Rating</b> - Still the same.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Re-read: 08.04.16</u>
</b><br>Oh no... I have sad news. I rated the book with one less star after re-reading. Don't get me wrong, it's still good, though not as good as it was the first time reading it, unfortunately :/<br><b>New rate</b>: 3 stars.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><u>First read review</u>:</b><br>Oh! I liked it better than the first one. Hope this continues :D <br><b>Rate</b>: 4 stars.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <a title="Sarah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah"><img alt="Sarah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388694025p2/3344685.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1477374780?book_show_action=true">Dec 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah">Sarah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780356500591" href="/book/show/11599179-blood-bound">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1477374780" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13411186838398861914"><b>1st Read May 2010</b><br/><b>2nd Read March 2014</b><br/><b>3rd Read December 2015</b> <br/><b>4th Read January 2017</b><br/><b>5th Read January 2018</b><br/><br/><b>Original Review</b><br/><br/><b>Blood Bound</b> continues the story about 6 months after the events of <b>Moon Called</b>. The werewolves have started to come out to the public, like the fae before them but the vampires are still keeping their existence a secret. When Mercy is woken by a phone call in the middle of the night from her vampire friend Stefan she isn't happy but Stefan needs a favor and as Mercy owes him one sh</span>
  <span id="freeText13411186838398861914" style="display:none"><b>1st Read May 2010</b><br /><b>2nd Read March 2014</b><br /><b>3rd Read December 2015</b> <br /><b>4th Read January 2017</b><br /><b>5th Read January 2018</b><br /><br /><b>Original Review</b><br /><br /><b>Blood Bound</b> continues the story about 6 months after the events of <b>Moon Called</b>. The werewolves have started to come out to the public, like the fae before them but the vampires are still keeping their existence a secret. When Mercy is woken by a phone call in the middle of the night from her vampire friend Stefan she isn't happy but Stefan needs a favor and as Mercy owes him one she agrees to help. There is a new vampire in the area who has raised Stefan's suspicion and he wants Mercy to be an impartial witness to the events by attending the meeting in her coyote form. It sounds like an easy way for Mercy to return the favor she owes Stefan but she should have realised things are never simple when it comes to vampires.<br /><br />I really enjoyed <b>Moon Called</b> but I thought that <b>Blood Bound</b> really stepped things up a gear. The first book focused more on the werewolves and setting the scene for the world <b>Patricia Briggs</b> has created. This book concentrates more on the vampires but because most of the characters are already established it gets to focus much more on the story. We get to learn more about Mercy's unique abilities as a Walker, abilities that are going to come in very handy in this book.<br /><br />Mercy has to show a lot of strength to face her enemies in <b>Blood Bound</b>, I'm really enjoying watching her character grow and of course you have her 2 werewolf admirers Adam &amp; Samuel still fighting for her attention. In fact she picks up another unexpected admirer in this book which I think is going to make the rest of the series even more interesting. Although this book focuses more on the vampires we still get to learn more about the werewolves. Although Mercy has a lot of allies she has to stand more on her own two feet and she has a major part to play in this installment. I'm hoping we continue to see her grow as a character throughout the rest of the series.<br /><br />I'd definitely recommend this series to urban fantasy fans. Mercy is a likeable heroine with unusual abilities in a genre that tends to focus more on vampires and werewolves (not that I have a problem with vamps &amp; weres but it is nice to come across something a little different). <b>Patricia Briggs</b> has created a believable world populated with interesting characters and this series really could end up taking you in any direction. I'm looking forward to reading more about Mercy and her friends.<br /><br />________________________________<br /><br /><b>2nd Read</b><br /><br />Buddy reread with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/871545761" rel="nofollow noopener">Ange</a><br /><br />I loved this just as much on my reread. Can't stop now, I've got to start the next book!<br /><br />________________________________<br /><br /><b>3rd Read</b><br /><br />Buddy read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/558210246" rel="nofollow noopener">Ange</a><br /><br />Since it's been nearly 2 years since Ange &amp; I buddy read this series last we decided we're well overdue another read in the run up to the release of Fire Touched next March.<br /><br />I love this series so much! The characters, the world building just everything about these books makes them a comfort read for me. Along with Ilona Andrews's Kate Daniels series this is probably my most reread series &amp; I never get tired of it.<br /><br />________________________________<br /><br /><b>4th Read</b><br /><br />I was supposed to be buddy reading this series with a group but I've been flying through this reread far too quickly! I can't help it with these books though, they just keep me totally hooked from beginning to end</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer33503591" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9202153632785939769">I enjoyed the second book in the series as well. There was one really creepy scene where a scary vampire was trying to get into Mercy's trailer at night while she was alone. There wasn't very much progression with Mercy's feelings toward Adam or Samuel but she does figure out some things. The action scenes were good and the story was fun to read. </span>

          </span>

<div id="review_97008304" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/97008304" />
    <a title="AH" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3255548-ah"><img alt="AH" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1275413869p2/3255548.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/97008304?book_show_action=true">Apr 04, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AH" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AH" href="/user/show/3255548-ah">AH</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=were">were</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=zzread-oct-2010">zzread-oct-2010</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3255548-ah?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer97008304" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9498465227543345989">This second book of Patricia Brigg’s Mercedes Thompson series did not disappoint. I thoroughly enjoyed every moment of this book. There was action, suspense, and the beginnings of a “love square” (as opposed to a love triangle).<br/><br/>There are so many aspects of this novel that I liked. I enjoyed the werewolf and vampire politics. I loved that Mercy was able to manoeuvre herself through the myriad of behaviors so that she would not offend or incite either werewolf or vampire. <br/><br/>A few more vampires are i</span>
  <span id="freeText9498465227543345989" style="display:none">This second book of Patricia Brigg’s Mercedes Thompson series did not disappoint. I thoroughly enjoyed every moment of this book. There was action, suspense, and the beginnings of a “love square” (as opposed to a love triangle).<br /><br />There are so many aspects of this novel that I liked. I enjoyed the werewolf and vampire politics. I loved that Mercy was able to manoeuvre herself through the myriad of behaviors so that she would not offend or incite either werewolf or vampire. <br /><br />A few more vampires are introduced, and we learn more about some of the others. Stefan becomes more and more likable with each book. Not only is he totally infatuated with all things Scooby Doo, but he is also a caring master of his human menagerie. Stefan also seems to be very attracted to Mercy. <br /><br />Mercy’s relationship with Adam continues to remain complicated. He has made her his mate in order to protect her. In werewolf politics, a mate holds the same rank, so Mercy is treated with the respect due to an Alpha. Mercy’s roommate Samuel still has feelings for her. It will be interesting to see who Mercy will choose.<br /><br />The villain in this book is so destructive and evil. A combination of vampire and demon, he is very powerful and able to mesmerize vampires. The werewolves take quite the battering from this character. <br /><br />There were several subplots that I did enjoy. I loved it when Mercy would talk to Mrs. Hanna’s ghost. She was a wonderfully quirky character and an interesting addition to the plot. I also liked how Mercy acted as a liaison between Tony from the local police department and the werewolves. <br /><br />I am really enjoying this series and I can’t wait to read the next book.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9498465227543345989" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('gvJW5x/ra8ifRpxcO6hcL2G5PK4ZL1ztzlaqsA/haC3VgBv2S/1TDcNC+ezqHj74yg2CH7YuQJ3CP56WQ7td4Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('FGdiTfCMA3MJ6ZMHHBKPXcctixmVMxLdADCMLzth8phDFS9cpJo7tlXt9rfNpO2KbJk1qDoyDq0MWbgJdzvHVA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer9395772880059846403"><i>Librarian Note: There is more than one author in the Goodreads database with this name.</i><br/><br/>Patricia Briggs was born in Butte, Montana, to a children’s librarian who passed on to her kids a love of reading and books. Patricia grew up reading fairy tales and books about horses, and later developed an interest in folklore and history. When she decided to write a book of her own, a fantasy book seemed a n</span>
  <span id="freeText9395772880059846403" style="display:none"><i>Librarian Note: There is more than one author in the Goodreads database with this name.</i><br /><br />Patricia Briggs was born in Butte, Montana, to a children’s librarian who passed on to her kids a love of reading and books. Patricia grew up reading fairy tales and books about horses, and later developed an interest in folklore and history. When she decided to write a book of her own, a fantasy book seemed a natural choice. Patricia graduated from Montana State University with degrees in history and German and she worked for a while as a substitute teacher. Currently, she lives in Montana with her husband, children, and six horses and writes full time, much to the delight of her fans.</span>
